ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年</a>　返游临安，真德秀为其诗题词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年7月27日</a>　七月二十七日，因真德秀所上劄子而有诗作。作品：《嘉定甲戌孟秋二十有七日，起居舍人兼直学士院真德秀上殿直前奏边事，不顾忌讳，一疏万言，援引古今，铺陈方略，忠谊感激，辞章浩瀚，诚有补于国家。天台戴复古获见此疏，伏读再三，窃有所感，敬效白乐天体以纪其事，录于野史》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_252497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252497?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252497'>榻前一奏一万字，历历写出忠义怀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252497'>顿首惶恐臣昧死，越录敢言天下事。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252497'>百年河洛行胡朔，恨满东南天一角。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252497'>夷甫诸人责未酬，志士愁眠剑锋落。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252497'>天意未回事难举，乡来一试成千误。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252497'>犬羊频岁自相屠，盛衰大抵由天数。<div id='poem_sentence_9_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_252497'>东风吹上妙高台，略望江淮见形势。<div id='poem_sentence_10_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_252497'>臣今未暇论规恢，胡虏已亡何虑哉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_252497'>更选人材，老练通达。<div id='poem_sentence_19_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_252497'>坐令国势九鼎重，所赖君心一点明。<div id='poem_sentence_22_252497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 湖州

桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3c589dda2b3c48838363b03f93d623e8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3c589dda2b3c48838363b03f93d623e8");'><span id='3c589dda2b3c48838363b03f93d623e8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1213&endYear=1213')">1213年</a>，47岁</div><div id='3c589dda2b3c48838363b03f93d623e8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1213&endYear=1213')">1213年</a>　乘舟游严州诸州县，沿桐江至武义。作品：《桐庐舟中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_252459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桐庐舟中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1213年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252459")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_252459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252459'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252459'>吴山青未了，桐江绿相迎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252459'>扁舟问何之，往访岩子陵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252459'>高风凛千古，卧蹴万乘主。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252459'>富贵直浮云，羊裘钓烟雨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252459'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_252459_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
武义
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='20fc538d0b06453a9a3de4e0271d3bba_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20fc538d0b06453a9a3de4e0271d3bba");'><span id='20fc538d0b06453a9a3de4e0271d3bba_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年1月</a>　正月，携诗访巩丰于武义，巩丰为其诗作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年</a>　与巩丰有诗唱和。作品：《栗斋巩仲至以元结文集为韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。）</span>《寄栗斋巩仲至》<span id='poem_sentence_0_252458'>寻常被酒时，归到急投枕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252458'>为爱次山文，今夜醉忘寝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252458'>伟哉浯溪碑，千载气凛凛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252458'>舂陵贼退篇，少陵犹敛衽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252458'>文章自一家，其意则古甚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252458'>大羹遗五味，纯素薄文锦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252458'>聱牙不同俗，斯人异所禀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252458'>君君望尧舜，人人欲仓廪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_252458'>古道不可行，时对窊樽饮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_252458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_252458'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_252458_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_252210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄栗斋巩仲至</a><span class='authorDate'>（1214年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_252210'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252210'>几度观朝报，差除不到君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252210'>山林自台阁，文字即功勋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252210_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252210'>吟苦孟东野，潜深杨子云。<div -----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3acc2b89895c4a84b9cd52bb53338883_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3acc2b89895c4a84b9cd52bb53338883");'><span id='3acc2b89895c4a84b9cd52bb53338883_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>至镇江府与史弥坚游，做喜雨楼诗。作品：《京口喜雨楼落成呈史固叔侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。刘丽玲《戴复古年谱》误系于嘉定八年。）</span><div id='poem_252429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京口喜雨楼落成呈史固叔侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1214年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_252429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252429'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252429'>京口画楼三百所，第一新楼名喜雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252429'>大鹏展翼到中天，化作檐楹不飞去。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252429'>一日登临天下奇，华灯照夜万琉璃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252429'>上与星辰共罗列，下映十里莲花池。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252429'>泰山为曲海为酿，手挈五湖为瓮盎。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252429'>银糟香沸碧瑶春，歌舞当垆多丽人。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252429'>使君歌了人皆饮，更赏谷中花似锦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252429'>五兵不用用酒兵，折冲樽俎边尘寝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_252429'>兹楼屹作东南美，孰识黄堂命名意。<div id='poem_sentence_8_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_252429'>特将此酒噀为霖，四海九州同一醉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_252429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_252429'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_252429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>于镇江府与李贾相识交游。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='43049003471b4c42ae097d5ae2e16ac4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("43049003471b4c42ae097d5ae2e16ac4");'><span -----title
仪征
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d976dd054e7e49c89062bc2daddce755_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d976dd054e7e49c89062bc2daddce755");'><span id='d976dd054e7e49c89062bc2daddce755_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1215&endYear=1215')">1215年</a>　或渡江至真州，与丰有俊游。作品：《贺新郎（丰真州建江淮伟观楼）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏词》）</span><div id='poem_252532' id='poem_sentence_0_252532'>百尺连云起。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252532'>试登临、江山人物，一时俱伟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252532'>旁挹金陵龙虎势，京岘诸峰对峙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252532'>隐隐接、扬州歌吹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252532'>雪浪舞从三峡下，乍逢迎、海若谈秋水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252532'>形胜地，有如此。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252532_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252532'>使君一世经纶志。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252532'>把风斤月斧，来此等闲游戏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_252532'>见说楼成无多日，大手一何容易。<div id='poem_sentence_8_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_252532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_252532'>人共乐，醉桃李。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_252532_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div -----detail
<div class='label1' id='fede9cadc65e480d8460789dc40e7c7e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fede9cadc65e480d8460789dc40e7c7e");'><span id='fede9cadc65e480d8460789dc40e7c7e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年</a>　秋，游鄂州访吴柔胜。作品：《湖北上吴胜之运使有感而言，非诗也》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_252483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖北上吴胜之运使有感而言非诗也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252483")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_252483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252483'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252483'>苍生积衅久，天欲尽杀之。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252483'>干戈杀不尽，继以大旱饥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252483'>田野委饿莩，道路纷流离。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252483'>众人识天意，不敢加扶持。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252483'>公怀佛子性，逆天救民命。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252483'>擅移太仓粟，众拂生尘甑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252483'>全活十万家，九州咏仁政。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252483'>逆天天弗怒，鬼神胡不恕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_252483'>白玉尚指瑕，青蝇工点素。<div id='poem_sentence_8_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_252483'>秋风动莼鲈，公亦思归去。<div id='poem_sentence_9_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_252483'>问公归去兮，苍生谁怙恃。<div id='poem_sentence_10_252483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_252483'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_252483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年9月9日</a>　重阳，与吴柔胜同登黄鹤楼。作品：《醉落魄（九日吴胜之运使黄鹤山登高）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏词》）</span><div id='poem_252551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>醉落魄 九日吴胜之运使黄鹤山登高</a><span class='authorDate'>（1216年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252551")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_252551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252551'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252551'>龙山行乐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252551'>何如今日登黄鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252551'>风光政要人酬酢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252551'>欲赋归来，莫是渊明错。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252551_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252551'>江山登览长如昨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252551'>飞鸿影里秋光薄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252551'>此怀祗有黄花觉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252551'>牢裹乌纱，一任西风作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_252551_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　秋至汉阳，与王中甫游。作品：《汉阳登览呈王中甫使君》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_251819' id='poem_sentence_5_252520'>岳王祠畔，杨柳烟锁古今愁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252520'>整顿乾坤手段，指授英雄方略，雅志若为酬。<div 星子
-----detail

-----title
分宜
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='905e25492912416489aa3bb2425f084d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("905e25492912416489aa3bb2425f084d");'><span id='905e25492912416489aa3bb2425f084d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1220&endYear=1220')">1220年</a>，54岁</div><div id='905e25492912416489aa3bb2425f084d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1220&endYear=1220')">1220年</a>　或游江西各地。作品：《题分宜县呈石子和知县》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_252338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题分宜县呈石子和知县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1220年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252338")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_252338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252338'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252338'>古镇更为县，封疆半是山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252338'>赋繁官吏窘，土瘠稻粱悭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252338'>流水心何急，高山意自闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252338'>春风细吹拂，桃李满民间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252338'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_252338_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
长沙

-----title
玉山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7389de4acdb541468e8281fd7c38fcb3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7389de4acdb541468e8281fd7c38fcb3");'><span id='7389de4acdb541468e8281fd7c38fcb3_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游江东信州玉山县，访赵蕃兄弟。作品：《章泉二老歌》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_252478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章泉二老歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252478")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_252478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252478'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252478'>在昔商山传四皓，又闻香山图九老。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252478'>异乡异姓适同时，争如章泉一家兄弟登耆颐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252478'>章泉之上两山下，有地可宫田可稼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252478'>伯也早休官，季也相约归林泉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252478'>名动京口耕谷口，山中有诗天下传。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252478'>一生得闲兼得寿，皓首庞眉世稀有。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252478'>竹隐先生八十三，定庵居士七十九。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252478'>客从远方来，亦是六十叟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_252478'>手把一枝梅，奉劝两翁酒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_252478'>问公何以致遐龄，请翁细说吾细听。<div id='poem_sentence_9_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_252478'>不烧丹，不学仙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_252478'>五行有常数，天所禀赋焉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_252478'>人生一气统四体，众人斲丧吾能全。<div id='poem_sentence_12_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_252478'>要知养生无他术，日多吃饭夜独眠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_252478'>承翁见教谢翁去，两翁慇勤留我住，是夜醉眠苔竹轩。<div id='poem_sentence_14_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_252478'>梦见山灵向我言，翁之所说皆不然。<div id='poem_sentence_15_252478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_252478'>两翁盛德合乎天，天与遐龄五百年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_252478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游江东信州玉山县，访赵蕃。作品：《玉山章泉本章氏所居，赵昌甫迁居于此，章泉之名遂显》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_251820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_251820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/251820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉山章泉本章氏所居赵昌甫迁居于此章泉之名遂显</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_251820")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_251820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_251820'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_251820'>兹山自开辟，有此一泓泉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_251820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_251820'>姓自章而立，名因赵以传。<div id='poem_sentence_1_251820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_251820'>源从番水出，地与瑞峰连。<div id='poem_sentence_2_251820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_251820'>寄语山中友，临流著数椽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_251820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_251820'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_251820_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ef1166a202c643758aa392ebf09aad33_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>，60岁</div><div id='ef1166a202c643758aa392ebf09aad33' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年12月</a>　十二月，离玉山。作品：《别章泉、定庵二老人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_251927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_251927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/251927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别章泉定庵二老人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_251927")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_251927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_251927'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_251927'>腊里春风转，埙篪一气和。<div id='poem_sentence_0_251927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_251927'>劝翁新岁酒，唱我老人歌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_251927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_251927'>一世声名重，四方书问多。<div id='poem_sentence_2_251927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_251927'>章泉一泓水，思与海同波。<div id='poem_sentence_3_251927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_251927'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_251927_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----end



-----title
广州
-----detail

古田

id='poem_sentence_3_251900'>人传花萼集，俱受水心知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_251900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_251900'></div><div "poem_title_251803")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_251803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_251803'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_251803'>客游花县自逍遥，百里风光在两桥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_251803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_251803'>语出桑阴鸠妇喜，身穿麦秀雉雏娇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_251803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_251803'>青山一任云来去，绿水多为风动摇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_251803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_251803_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
莆田（兴化军）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='28356b3ea92f45b0a5672fb18495b6f5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("28356b3ea92f45b0a5672fb18495b6f5");'><span id='28356b3ea92f45b0a5672fb18495b6f5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1230&endYear=1230')">1230年</a>，64岁</div><div id='28356b3ea92f45b0a5672fb18495b6f5' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
邵武
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3bc90595e7214f7da06c8d1279033348_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3bc90595e7214f7da06c8d1279033348");'><span id='3bc90595e7214f7da06c8d1279033348_link' 赣州

id='poem_sentence_2_252408'>玉华东西岩，具体而微者。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252408'>神功巧穿凿，石壁生<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_4_252408'>玲珑透风月，宜冬复宜夏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_252408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_252408'>中有补陀仙，坐断此潇洒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_252408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_252408'>空山茅苇区，无地可税驾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_252408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_252408'>举目忽此逢，心骇见希诧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_252408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_252408'>题诗愧不能，行人亦无暇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_252408_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_252408'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_252408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游广西，有诗。作品：《市舶提举管仲登饮于万贡堂有诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_252406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>市舶提举管仲登饮于万贡堂有诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252406")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_252406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252406'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252406'>七十老翁头雪白，落在江湖卖诗册。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252406'>平生知己管夷吾，得为万贡堂前客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252406'>嘲吟有罪遭天厄，谋归未办资身策。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252406'>鸡林莫有买诗人，明日烦公问蕃舶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252406'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_252406_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
新余（新建）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9009366d9bd74c4b90970e12b8354e5b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9009366d9bd74c4b90970e12b8354e5b");'><span id='9009366d9bd74c4b90970e12b8354e5b_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　过渝江，访李贾。作品：《绿阴亭自唐时有之，到今五百年，卢肇二三公题诗之后，吟声寂寂久矣，亭前古木不存，绿阴之名殆成虚设。今诗人李贾友山作尉于此，实居此亭，公事之暇，与江山风景应接，境因人胜，见于吟笔多矣，友人石屏戴复古访之，相与周旋于亭上，题四绝句以记曾来》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_251673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_251673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/251673?labeling=true' class='authorDate'>（1236年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　与萧元之兄弟游，有诗作。作品：《题渝江萧氏园亭 体仁、体信伯仲，佳士也。一区同居，不出户庭而得溪山之胜。自昔有秀江亭，山谷先生尝留题云，澄波古木，使人得意于尘垢之外。盖人闲景幽，两奇绝耳。所题之壁犹存（一作“体仁、体信，佳公子也。一区同居，乡里称善，石屏见而喜之，为题三诗。”）》3首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_252361' class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_251808")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_251808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_251808'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_251808'>龙墀射策三千字，未抵胸中十万兵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_251808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_251808'>远大无过为将相，文章争似立功名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_251808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_251808'>当今天下几豪杰，独数君家两弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_251808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_251808'>世事从横人事左，未知何以措升平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_251808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_251808'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_251808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　见宋自逊，宋作词以送之。作品：《沁园春（送戴石屏）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《中兴以来绝妙词选》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_471720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_471720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/471720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春 送戴石屏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24639, "宋", "宋自逊", "poem_title_471720")'>宋自逊</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_471720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_471720'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_471720'>归去来兮，田园将芜，云胡不归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_471720'>既有诗千首，如斯者少，行年七十，从古来稀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_471720'>地阙东南，天倾西北，人事何缘有足时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_471720'>江湖上，转不如前日，步步危机。<div id='poem_sentence_3_471720_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_471720'>石屏自有柴扉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_471720'>占海岸、潮头岸一矶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_471720'>唤䌽衣孙子，携壶挈榼，白头翁媪，举案齐眉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_471720'>身外声名，世间梦幻，万事一酲无是非。<div id='poem_sentence_7_471720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_471720'>书来往，都不须长语，直写心期。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_471720_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　在平江诗友聚会，有诗论之。作品：《诸诗人会于吴门翁际可通判席上，高菊涧有诗，仆有“客星聚吴会，诗派落松江”之句，方子万使君喜之，遂足成篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋·戴复古《石屏诗集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_252157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_252157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/252157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸诗人会于吴门翁际可通判席上高菊涧有诗仆有客星聚吴会诗派落松江之句方子万使君喜之遂足成篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26391, "南宋", "戴复古", "poem_title_252157")'>戴复古</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_252157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_252157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_252157'>客星聚吴会，诗派落松江。<div id='poem_sentence_0_252157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_252157'>老眼洞千古，旷怀开八窗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_252157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_252157'>风流谈夺席，歌笑酒盈缸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_252157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_252157'>杨陆不再作，何人可受降。<div id='poem_sentence_3_252157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_252157'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_252157_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
